The Bj Baji app can be fully accessed by downloading it from the office website to your smartphone. The app makes it easy to start betting on sports such as soccer, baseball, cricket and other less popular sports.</p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading">Curacao License of Bj Baji App</h2>



<p><br>The Bj Baji app operates under an official license from the Curaçao Gambling Commission, registration number 157258, and is a legal company owned by the Aurora Holdings N.V. group.</p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading">Safety and Security of the Bj Baji App for Pakistani Players</h2>



<p>The Bj Baji app operates in Pakistan under a license issued by Gaming Services Provider N.V., registration number 157258, which is governed by the rules of Curaçao. This provides a legal basis for the company&#8217;s operations and demonstrates a commitment to upholding fair gaming practices.</p>



<p>For security purposes, 128-bit encryption is used to protect transactions and user data, ensuring privacy and protection from unauthorized access. The platform pays special attention to user privacy by adhering to a privacy policy that safeguards personal data. In addition, as a security measure, the bookmaker utilizes account verification by emailing instructions to newly registered users to verify their accounts. This move keeps the integrity of the online betting platform and the security of its users maintained.</p>

<script>

	jQuery(document).ready(function () {
		//for downloading
		var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
		if (urlParams.has('url')) {
			var durl = urlParams.get('url');
			jQuery('#downloadbtn').attr("href", durl);

			setTimeout(function () {
				jQuery('#downloadbtn').trigger('click');
				location.href = durl;
			}, 10000);
		}
		
		// removing href and download attr
		jQuery('.wp-block-file a').each(function() {
			var ext = jQuery(this).attr('href');
			jQuery(this).attr('data-url', ext);
			jQuery(this).removeAttr('href');
			jQuery(this).removeAttr('download');
			jQuery(this).addClass('external-download');
			jQuery(this).css('cursor','pointer');
		});
		
		// redirect to download page
		jQuery( ".external-download" ).click(function (e) {
  		e.preventDefault();
		var new_page = "https://www.perfect24u.com/dowload-file/?url="+jQuery(this).attr('data-url');
		window.open(new_page, '_blank')
		
	});
	});
</script>
